WARNING: Does not account for THIS calls.
You will need to manually edit the non-static functions
eg: Camera_set_FieldOfView only takes a float, but the
first paramater technically needs to be an IntPtr, which
is the Cameras Memory Address of which you plan
to apply the FOV Change.

Paramater names are not present, so you
will need to manually figure it out :)
